<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports screen readers</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Limits the number of visible toasts</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Handles promise lifecycles</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Pauses on hover, focus, or page idle</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports programmatic update/remove</li>
</ul>

</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 4. Wrap your app with the toaster --&gt;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>script</span> <span class="token attr-name">lang</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>ts<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token maybe-class-name">Toaster</span></span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;./toaster.svelte&quot;</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript"></span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>script</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>Toaster</span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 5. Within your app --&gt;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token attr-name">onclick=</span><span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token language-javascript">    toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">create</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Hello&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">    Add top-right toast
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>button</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token attr-name">onclick=</span><span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token language-javascript">    toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">create</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Data submitted!&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;success&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">    Success toast
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>button</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<p>To use toast effectively, understand these key parts:</p>
<h3 id="toast-group" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Toast Group<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#toast-group"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">
<p><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toast.group.machine</code> - State machine logic for the toast region.</p>
</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">
<p><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toast.group.connect</code> - Maps group state to JSX props and subscriptions.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>We recommend setting up the toast group machine once at the root of your
project.</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="toast-item" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Toast Item<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#toast-item"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toast.machine</code> - State machine logic for a single toast.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toast.connect</code> - Maps toast state to JSX props and controls.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="creating-a-toast" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Creating a toast<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#creating-a-toast"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Common toast types are <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">info</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">success</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">warning</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loading</code>, and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">error</code>. You
can also pass a custom type string.</p>
<p>Helper methods are also available: <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.info(...)</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.success(...)</code>,
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.warning(...)</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.error(...)</code>, and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.loading(...)</code>.</p>
<p>To create a toast, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.create(...)</code> method.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">create</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Hello World&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;This is a toast&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;info&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The options you can pass in are:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">title</code> — The title of the toast.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">description</code> — The description of the toast.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">type</code> — The type of the toast. Can be either <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">error</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">success</code> , <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">info</code>,
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">warning</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loading</code>, or any custom string.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">duration</code> — The duration of the toast. The default duration is computed based
on the specified <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">type</code>.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStatusChange</code> — A callback that listens for the status changes across the
toast lifecycle.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">removeDelay</code> — The delay before unmounting the toast from the DOM. Useful for
transition.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">action</code> — Optional action button with <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">label</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onClick</code>.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closable</code> — Whether to render a close trigger.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="changing-the-placement" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Changing the placement<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-placement"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Placement is configured on the toast store and applies to the whole toast group.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> toaster <span class="token operator">=</span> toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">createStore</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">placement</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;top-start&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="overlapping-toasts" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Overlapping toasts<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#overlapping-toasts"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>When multiple toasts are created, they are rendered in a stack. To make the
toasts overlap, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">overlap</code> property to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> toaster <span class="token operator">=</span> toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">createStore</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">overlap</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Be sure to set up the <a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px" href="#requirement">required styles</a> to make overlap work
correctly.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 id="changing-the-duration" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Changing the duration<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-duration"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Every toast has a default visible duration depending on the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">type</code> set. Here&#x27;s
the following toast types and matching default durations:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>type</th><th>duration</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">info</code></td><td><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_sm ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400">5000</code></td></tr><tr><td><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">error</code></td><td><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_sm ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400">5000</code></td></tr><tr><td><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">success</code></td><td><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_sm ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400">2000</code></td></tr><tr><td><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loading</code></td><td><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_sm ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400">Infinity</code></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>You can override the duration of the toast by passing the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">duration</code> property to
the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.create(...)</code> function.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">create</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Hello World&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;This is a toast&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;info&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">duration</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">6000</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.create(...)</code> for new toasts and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.update(id, ...)</code> to modify
an existing one.</p>
<h2 id="using-portals" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Using portals<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#using-portals"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Using a portal is helpful to ensure that the toast is rendered outside the DOM
hierarchy of the parent component. To render the toast in a portal, wrap the
rendered toasts in the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ToastProvider</code> within your framework-specific portal.</p>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token each"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token keyword">/each</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<h2 id="programmatic-control" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Programmatic control<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-control"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To update a toast programmatically, you need access to the unique identifier of
the toast.</p>
<p>This identifier can be either:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> passed into <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.create(...)</code> or,</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">the returned random <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> when the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.create(...)</code> is called.</li>
</ul>
<p>You can use any of the following methods to control a toast:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.update(...)</code> — Updates a toast.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.remove(...)</code> — Removes a toast instantly without delay.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.dismiss(...)</code> — Removes a toast with delay.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.pause(...)</code> — Pauses a toast.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.resume(...)</code> — Resumes a toast.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.isVisible(...)</code> — Checks if a toast is currently visible.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.isDismissed(...)</code> — Checks if a toast has been dismissed.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// grab the id from the created toast</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> id <span class="token operator">=</span> toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">create</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Hello World&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;This is a toast&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;info&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">duration</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">6000</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// update the toast</span>
</span><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">update</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>id<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Hello World&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;This is a toast&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;success&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// remove the toast</span>
</span><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">remove</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>id<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// dismiss the toast</span>
</span><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">dismiss</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>id<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="pause-and-resume-all-toasts" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Pause and resume all toasts<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#pause-and-resume-all-toasts"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Call <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pause()</code>/<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">resume()</code> without an <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to affect all active toasts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">pause</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">resume</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="handling-promises" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Handling promises<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#handling-promises"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The toast group API exposes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.promise()</code> function to allow you update
the toast when it resolves or rejects.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>With the promise API, you can pass the toast options for each promise
lifecycle. <strong>The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loading</code> option is required</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">promise</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>promise<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">loading</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Loading&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Please wait...&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">success</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">data</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Success&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Your request has been completed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">error</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">err</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Error&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;An error has occurred&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.promise(...)</code> returns <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">{ id, unwrap }</code>, so you can await the original
result:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> result <span class="token operator">=</span> toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">promise</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token function">fetchData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">loading</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Loading...&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword control-flow">await</span> result<span class="token operator">?.</span><span class="token method function property-access">unwrap</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="pausing-the-toasts" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Pausing the toasts<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#pausing-the-toasts"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>There are three scenarios that pause toast timeout:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">When a user hovers or focuses the toast region.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">When the document loses focus or the page is idle (e.g. switching to a new
browser tab), controlled via the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pauseOnPageIdle</code> store option.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">When the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.pause(id)</code> is called.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Global pause options</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> toaster <span class="token operator">=</span> toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">createStore</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">pauseOnPageIdle</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Programmatically pause a toast (by `id`)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// `id` is the return value of `toaster.create(...)`</span>
</span><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">pause</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>id<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="limiting-the-number-of-toasts" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Limiting the number of toasts<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#limiting-the-number-of-toasts"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Toasts are great but displaying too many of them can sometimes hamper the user
experience. To limit visible toasts, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">max</code> on the store.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> toaster <span class="token operator">=</span> toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">createStore</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">max</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="focus-hotkey-for-toasts" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Focus Hotkey for toasts<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focus-hotkey-for-toasts"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>When a toast is created, you can focus the toast region by pressing the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">alt + T</code>. This is useful for screen readers and keyboard navigation.</p>
<p>Set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">hotkey</code> store option to change the underlying hotkey.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">group</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">store</span><span class="token operator">:</span> toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">createStore</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">hotkey</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;F6&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="listening-for-toast-lifecycle" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Listening for toast lifecycle<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-toast-lifecycle"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>When a toast is created, you can listen for the status changes across its
lifecycle using the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onStatusChange</code> callback when you call
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toaster.create(...)</code>.</p>
<p>The status values are:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">visible</code> - The toast is mounted and rendered</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dismissing</code> - The toast is closing but still mounted</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">unmounted</code> - The toast has been completely unmounted and no longer exists</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">toaster<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">info</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Hello World&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;This is a toast&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;info&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">onStatusChange</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { status: &quot;visible&quot; | &quot;dismissing&quot; | &quot;unmounted&quot; }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Toast status:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="changing-the-gap-between-toasts" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Changing the gap between toasts<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-gap-between-toasts"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>When multiple toasts are rendered, a gap of <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">16px</code> is applied between each
toast. To change this value, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">gap</code> on the store.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> toaster <span class="token operator">=</span> toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">createStore</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">gap</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">24</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="changing-the-offset" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Changing the offset<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-offset"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The toast region has a default <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">1rem</code> offset from the viewport. Use the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">offsets</code> store option to change this offset.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> toaster <span class="token operator">=</span> toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">createStore</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">offsets</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;24px&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="requirement" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Requirement<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#requirement"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The toast machine injects a bunch of css variables that are required for it to
work. You need to connect these variables in your styles.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">translate</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--x</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--y</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">scale</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--scale</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">z-index</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--z-index</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">height</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--height</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">opacity</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">var</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token variable">--opacity</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">will-change</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> translate<span class="token punctuation">,</span> opacity<span class="token punctuation">,</span> scale<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>To make transitions smooth, include <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">transition</code> properties.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">transition</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    translate <span class="token number">400</span><span class="token unit">ms</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    scale <span class="token number">400</span><span class="token unit">ms</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    opacity <span class="token number">400</span><span class="token unit">ms</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">transition-timing-function</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">cubic-bezier</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0.21</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1.02</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0.73</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">transition</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    translate <span class="token number">400</span><span class="token unit">ms</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    scale <span class="token number">400</span><span class="token unit">ms</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    opacity <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token unit">ms</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">transition-timing-function</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token function">cubic-bezier</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0.06</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0.71</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0.55</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="toast-styling" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Toast styling<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#toast-styling"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a toast is created and the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getRootProps()</code> from the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toast.connect</code> is
used, the toast will have a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-type</code> that matches the specified <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">type</code> at its
creation.</p>
<p>You can use this property to style the toast.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-type</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;info&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for the specific toast type */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-type</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;error&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-type</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;success&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The toast&#x27;s <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getCount</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; number</code><span class="d_block">The total number of toasts</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getToasts</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ToastProps&lt;any&gt;[]</code><span class="d_block">The toasts</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">subscribe</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(callback: (toasts: Options&lt;O&gt;[]) =&gt; void) =&gt; VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Subscribe to the toast group</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<h3 id="css-variables" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">CSS Variables<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#css-variables"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

id=\"toast/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the toast anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"toast\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the toast package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as toast from \"@zag-js/toast\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"toast/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo use toast effectively, understand these key parts:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eToast Group\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoast.group.machine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic for the toast region.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoast.group.connect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps group state to JSX props and subscriptions.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWe recommend setting up the toast group machine once at the root of your\nproject.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eToast Item\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoast.machine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic for a single toast.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoast.connect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps toast state to JSX props and controls.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eCreating a toast\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCommon toast types are \u003ccode\u003einfo\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003esuccess\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ewarning\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eloading\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003eerror\u003c/code\u003e. You\ncan also pass a custom type string.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eHelper methods are also available: \u003ccode\u003etoaster.info(...)\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etoaster.success(...)\u003c/code\u003e,\n\u003ccode\u003etoaster.warning(...)\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etoaster.error(...)\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003etoaster.loading(...)\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo create a toast, use the \u003ccode\u003etoaster.create(...)\u003c/code\u003e method.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003etoaster.create({\n  title: \"Hello World\",\n  description: \"This is a toast\",\n  type: \"info\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe options you can pass in are:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etitle\u003c/code\u003e — The title of the toast.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edescription\u003c/code\u003e — The description of the toast.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e — The type of the toast. Can be either \u003ccode\u003eerror\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003esuccess\u003c/code\u003e , \u003ccode\u003einfo\u003c/code\u003e,\n\u003ccode\u003ewarning\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eloading\u003c/code\u003e, or any custom string.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eduration\u003c/code\u003e — The duration of the toast. The default duration is computed based\non the specified \u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonStatusChange\u003c/code\u003e — A callback that listens for the status changes across the\ntoast lifecycle.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eremoveDelay\u003c/code\u003e — The delay before unmounting the toast from the DOM. Useful for\ntransition.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaction\u003c/code\u003e — Optional action button with \u003ccode\u003elabel\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonClick\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eclosable\u003c/code\u003e — Whether to render a close trigger.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eChanging the placement\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePlacement is configured on the toast store and applies to the whole toast group.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst toaster = toast.createStore({\n  placement: \"top-start\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eOverlapping toasts\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen multiple toasts are created, they are rendered in a stack. To make the\ntoasts overlap, set the \u003ccode\u003eoverlap\u003c/code\u003e property to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst toaster = toast.createStore({\n  overlap: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBe sure to set up the \u003ca href=\"#requirement\"\u003erequired styles\u003c/a\u003e to make overlap work\ncorrectly.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eChanging the duration\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEvery toast has a default visible duration depending on the \u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e set. Here's\nthe following toast types and matching default durations:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026#x3C;PropValueTable\nitems={{\nheadings: [\"type\", \"duration\"],\ndata: [\n[\"info\", \"5000\"],\n[\"error\", \"5000\"],\n[\"success\", \"2000\"],\n[\"loading\", \"Infinity\"],\n],\n}}\n/\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can override the duration of the toast by passing the \u003ccode\u003eduration\u003c/code\u003e property to\nthe \u003ccode\u003etoaster.create(...)\u003c/code\u003e function.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{5}\"\u003etoaster.create({\n  title: \"Hello World\",\n  description: \"This is a toast\",\n  type: \"info\",\n  duration: 6000,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003etoaster.create(...)\u003c/code\u003e for new toasts and \u003ccode\u003etoaster.update(id, ...)\u003c/code\u003e to modify\nan existing one.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsing portals\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUsing a portal is helpful to ensure that the toast is rendered outside the DOM\nhierarchy of the parent component. To render the toast in a portal, wrap the\nrendered toasts in the \u003ccode\u003eToastProvider\u003c/code\u003e within your framework-specific portal.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"toast/using-portal.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eProgrammatic control\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo update a toast programmatically, you need access to the unique identifier of\nthe toast.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis identifier can be either:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ethe \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e passed into \u003ccode\u003etoaster.create(...)\u003c/code\u003e or,\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ethe returned random \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e when the \u003ccode\u003etoaster.create(...)\u003c/code\u003e is called.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can use any of the following methods to control a toast:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoaster.update(...)\u003c/code\u003e — Updates a toast.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoaster.remove(...)\u003c/code\u003e — Removes a toast instantly without delay.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoaster.dismiss(...)\u003c/code\u003e — Removes a toast with delay.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoaster.pause(...)\u003c/code\u003e — Pauses a toast.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoaster.resume(...)\u003c/code\u003e — Resumes a toast.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoaster.isVisible(...)\u003c/code\u003e — Checks if a toast is currently visible.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoaster.isDismissed(...)\u003c/code\u003e — Checks if a toast has been dismissed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2,11-15}\"\u003e// grab the id from the created toast\nconst id = toaster.create({\n  title: \"Hello World\",\n  description: \"This is a toast\",\n  type: \"info\",\n  duration: 6000,\n})\n\n// update the toast\ntoaster.update(id, {\n  title: \"Hello World\",\n  description: \"This is a toast\",\n  type: \"success\",\n})\n\n// remove the toast\ntoaster.remove(id)\n\n// dismiss the toast\ntoaster.dismiss(id)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003ePause and resume all toasts\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCall \u003ccode\u003epause()\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eresume()\u003c/code\u003e without an \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to affect all active toasts.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003etoaster.pause()\ntoaster.resume()\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eHandling promises\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe toast group API exposes a \u003ccode\u003etoaster.promise()\u003c/code\u003e function to allow you update\nthe toast when it resolves or rejects.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWith the promise API, you can pass the toast options for each promise\nlifecycle. \u003cstrong\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003eloading\u003c/code\u003e option is required\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003etoaster.promise(promise, {\n  loading: {\n    title: \"Loading\",\n    description: \"Please wait...\",\n  },\n  success: (data) =\u003e ({\n    title: \"Success\",\n    description: \"Your request has been completed\",\n  }),\n  error: (err) =\u003e ({\n    title: \"Error\",\n    description: \"An error has occurred\",\n  }),\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003etoaster.promise(...)\u003c/code\u003e returns \u003ccode\u003e{ id, unwrap }\u003c/code\u003e, so you can await the original\nresult:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst result = toaster.promise(fetchData(), {\n  loading: { title: \"Loading...\" },\n})\nawait result?.unwrap()\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003ePausing the toasts\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThere are three scenarios that pause toast timeout:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWhen a user hovers or focuses the toast region.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWhen the document loses focus or the page is idle (e.g. switching to a new\nbrowser tab), controlled via the \u003ccode\u003epauseOnPageIdle\u003c/code\u003e store option.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWhen the \u003ccode\u003etoaster.pause(id)\u003c/code\u003e is called.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e// Global pause options\nconst toaster = toast.createStore({\n  pauseOnPageIdle: true,\n})\n\n// Programmatically pause a toast (by `id`)\n// `id` is the return value of `toaster.create(...)`\ntoaster.pause(id)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eLimiting the number of toasts\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eToasts are great but displaying too many of them can sometimes hamper the user\nexperience. To limit visible toasts, set \u003ccode\u003emax\u003c/code\u003e on the store.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{3}\"\u003econst toaster = toast.createStore({\n  max: 10,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eFocus Hotkey for toasts\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen a toast is created, you can focus the toast region by pressing the\n\u003ccode\u003ealt + T\u003c/code\u003e. This is useful for screen readers and keyboard navigation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet the \u003ccode\u003ehotkey\u003c/code\u003e store option to change the underlying hotkey.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(toast.group.machine, {\n  store: toast.createStore({ hotkey: [\"F6\"] }),\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eListening for toast lifecycle\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen a toast is created, you can listen for the status changes across its\nlifecycle using the \u003ccode\u003eonStatusChange\u003c/code\u003e callback when you call\n\u003ccode\u003etoaster.create(...)\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe status values are:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evisible\u003c/code\u003e - The toast is mounted and rendered\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edismissing\u003c/code\u003e - The toast is closing but still mounted\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eunmounted\u003c/code\u003e - The toast has been completely unmounted and no longer exists\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{3-7}\"\u003etoaster.info({\n  title: \"Hello World\",\n  description: \"This is a toast\",\n  type: \"info\",\n  onStatusChange: (details) =\u003e {\n    // details =\u003e { status: \"visible\" | \"dismissing\" | \"unmounted\" }\n    console.log(\"Toast status:\", details)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eChanging the gap between toasts\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen multiple toasts are rendered, a gap of \u003ccode\u003e16px\u003c/code\u003e is applied between each\ntoast. To change this value, set \u003ccode\u003egap\u003c/code\u003e on the store.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst toaster = toast.createStore({\n  gap: 24,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eChanging the offset\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe toast region has a default \u003ccode\u003e1rem\u003c/code\u003e offset from the viewport. Use the\n\u003ccode\u003eoffsets\u003c/code\u003e store option to change this offset.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst toaster = toast.createStore({\n  offsets: \"24px\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eStyling guide\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eRequirement\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe toast machine injects a bunch of css variables that are required for it to\nwork. You need to connect these variables in your styles.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"root\"] {\n  translate: var(--x) var(--y);\n  scale: var(--scale);\n  z-index: var(--z-index);\n  height: var(--height);\n  opacity: var(--opacity);\n  will-change: translate, opacity, scale;\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo make transitions smooth, include \u003ccode\u003etransition\u003c/code\u003e properties.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"root\"] {\n  transition:\n    translate 400ms,\n    scale 400ms,\n    opacity 400ms;\n  transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.21, 1.02, 0.73, 1);\n}\n\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-state=\"closed\"] {\n  transition:\n    translate 400ms,\n    scale 400ms,\n    opacity 200ms;\n  transition-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.06, 0.71, 0.55, 1);\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eToast styling\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen a toast is created and the \u003ccode\u003eapi.getRootProps()\u003c/code\u003e from the \u003ccode\u003etoast.connect\u003c/code\u003e is\nused, the toast will have a \u003ccode\u003edata-type\u003c/code\u003e that matches the specified \u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e at its\ncreation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can use this property to style the toast.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"root\"][data-type=\"info\"] {\n  /* Styles for the specific toast type
